# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Tensor form factors of the $Δ^+$ baryon induced by isovector and isoscalar currents in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12360)
*Z. Asmaee,N. Hajirasouliha,K. Azizi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了Δ+重子的张量形状因子，通过张量流的矩阵元定义，描述其内部结构和自旋分布。文章给出了Δ+到Δ+张量流矩阵元的完整洛伦兹分解，并分析了同位旋矢量和同位旋标量张量流对应的形状因子差异，反映了Δ+重子中上下夸克组分的不同贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Δ+重子的内部结构和自旋分布，探究其夸克组分的贡献差异。

Method: 通过洛伦兹分解方法，结合洛伦兹协变性、Rarita-Schwinger约束和时间反演对称性，分析Δ+→Δ+张量流矩阵元。

Result: 获得了完整的洛伦兹分解形式，发现了同位旋矢量和同位旋标量张量流形状因子之间的差异。

Conclusion: 上下夸克在Δ+重子中的贡献不同，张量形状因子能有效反映这种差异。

Abstract: The tensor form factors of the $Δ^+$ baryon are defined through the matrix element of the tensor current and describe its internal structure and spin distribution. We present the full Lorentz decomposition for the $Δ^+ \rightarrow Δ^+$ tensor current matrix element, including all independent structures consistent with Lorentz covariance, the Rarita-Schwinger constraints, and time-reversal symmetry. By investigating the tensor form factors corresponding to both the isovector and isoscalar tensor currents, we observed differences that reflect the distinct contributions of up and down quark components in the $Δ^+$ baryon.

</details>


### [2] [Divergences in the hadronic light-by-light amplitude of the holographic soft-wall model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11797)
*Josef Leutgeb,Jonas Mager,Anton Rebhan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文使用WKB近似方法研究了一类全息软墙模型中的发散和极限不交换问题，发现涉及Chern-Simons项的可观测量（如VVA关联函数和强子光-by-光散射张量）的单共振求和不收敛。部分问题可通过直接在五维框架中使用体-边界传播子避免，但强子光-by-光散射张量在五维形式下仍发散，导致无法正确实现短距约束并使μ子g-2贡献发散。文章还讨论了可解决此问题的软墙模型修正方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示全息软墙模型中由于极限不交换导致的发散问题，特别是在涉及Chern-Simons项的物理量计算中的表现，并寻求可行的修正方案。

Method: 采用WKB近似方法分析软墙模型，比较四维共振求和与五维体-边界传播子方法，检验不同极限下的收敛性。

Result: 发现VVA关联函数和强子光-by-光散射张量在共振求和下不收敛；VVA问题可通过五维方法规避，但强子光-by-光散射在五维下仍发散，导致μ子g-2发散；提出可修复该问题的软墙模型改进方案。

Conclusion: 标准软墙模型在处理某些非perturbative QCD效应时存在根本性发散问题，需通过模型修正才能正确描述短距行为和精确计算如muon g-2等关键观测量。

Abstract: We use the WKB approximation to uncover divergences and instances of non-commuting limits in a large class of holographic soft-wall models. We show that the infinite sum over single resonance contributions for a variety of observables involving the Chern-Simons term, such as the VVA correlator or the hadronic light-by-light tensor, does not converge. These divergences can in some cases (such as the VVA correlator) be traced back to non-commuting limits and avoided by working directly in the 5-dimensional setup with bulk-to-boundary propagators. However, the hadronic light-by-light scattering tensor also diverges in the 5-dimensional formulation with corresponding Green functions, preventing a correct implementation of the Melnikov-Vainshtein short-distance constraint and even leading to an infinite contribution to the muon $g-2$. We also discuss modifications of the standard soft-wall model that are able to resolve this issue.

</details>


### [3] [The one-jettiness distribution contains super-super-leading logarithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11799)
*Andrea Banfi,Jeffrey R. Forshaw,Jack Holguin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现，在单色子加喷注产生过程中，一喷注度（τ₁）在相对于Born水平的αₛ⁴ ln(1/τ₁)⁶阶出现超前导对数，比之前已知的任何超前导对数多一个对数项。这一额外对数不伴随额外极点，因此与在尺度τ₁Q处普适部分子分布函数的因子化一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高能物理中喷注产生过程的高阶辐射修正，特别是探索是否存在未被识别的超前导对数效应，以完善理论预测精度。

Method: 通过分析一喷注度（τ₁）在色单态加喷注过程中的行为，结合因子化理论和对数发散结构的研究，识别出新的超前导对数项。

Result: 发现了在αₛ⁴ ln(1/τ₁)⁶阶的新超前导对数，其主导程度超过以往已知的超前导对数，并验证了其与部分子分布函数因子化的兼容性。

Conclusion: 一喷注度在该过程中存在更强的超前导对数效应，但该效应不破坏因子化结构，表明传统因子化框架仍适用于描述此类高阶对数。

Abstract: We show that one-jettiness ($τ_1$) in colour-singlet plus jet production suffers from super-leading logarithms starting at order $α_{\mathrm s}^4 \ln(1/τ_1)^6$ relative to the Born level. This is one logarithm more dominant than any previously identified super-leading logarithms. The extra logarithm is not associated with additional poles, and is therefore consistent with the factorization of universal parton distribution functions at scale $τ_1 Q$, where $Q$ is the hard scale.

</details>


### [4] [First bounds on effective muon interactions using the NA64$μ$ experiment at CERN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11801)
*Paolo Crivelli,Josu Hernandez-Garcia,Jacobo Lopez-Pavon,Victor Martin Lozano,Laura Molina Bueno*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了NA64μ实验在SMEFT和νSMEFT框架下对未受限制的四费米子算符的探测能力，填补了当前实验与未来μ子对撞机之间的新物理探索空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于轻中微子质量和轻子混合现象的存在，扩展的有效场论（如νSMEFT）具有理论动机，而现有实验对某些四费米子算符缺乏约束，需通过NA64μ等实验填补空白。

Method: 通过分析NA64μ实验数据，研究其在SMEFT和νSMEFT框架下对未受限制的四费米子算符的约束能力，并计算当前领先界限及未来灵敏度。

Result: NA64μ可探测此前完全未受限制的两个SMEFT四轻子算符并打破现有平坦方向；在νSMEFT中可约束三个未受限制的四费米子算符，并给出了当前最严格的界限及未来灵敏度预测。

Conclusion: NA64μ实验在SMEFT和νSMEFT框架下具有独特的新物理探测潜力，能够填补当前实验与未来高能设施之间的空白，为新物理研究提供重要补充。

Abstract: We analyze how NA64$μ$ can contribute to the global SMEFT program demonstrating that it can probe two effective four lepton operators completely unbounded so far and break one of the current flat directions. Furthermore, we also study an extension of SMEFT that includes fermion singlets of the SM gauge group in the low energy field content. This effective field theory, usually dubbed $ν$SMEFT, is well motivated by the observation of light neutrino masses and leptonic mixing. We find that NA64$μ$ can constrain three unbounded four fermion operators of the $ν$SMEFT. We derive the current leading bounds on these operators and compute the future sensitivity. Our results fill the gap between the current experimental program and a possible future muon collider able to probe this type of New Physics.

</details>


### [5] [Photon-induced jet production at future lepton colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11812)
*Thomas Gehrmann,Peter Meinzinger*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 研究高能正负电子碰撞中光子诱导的喷注产生过程，特别是其对解析光子结构贡献的评估潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解析光子的部分子内容目前实验数据约束较弱，需通过喷注产生过程进一步研究。

Method: 对光子诱导的喷注产生过程进行详细的唯象学研究。

Result: 揭示了这些过程在评估解析光子结构贡献方面的潜力。

Conclusion: 高能e+e-碰撞中的喷注产生有助于约束光子的内部结构。

Abstract: The production of hadronic final states in electron-positron or electron-hadron collisions is induced predominantly by quasi-real photons that were emitted off incoming leptons. In these processes, the photon either enters directly or through its resolved parton content, which is at present only loosely constrained by experimental data. We perform a detailed phenomenological study of photon-induced jet production processes in high-energy $e^+e^-$ collisions, investigating in particular their potential to assess contributions from the resolved photon structure.

</details>


### [6] [The weak decay constant of positronium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11839)
*Milena Piotrowska,Francesco Giacosa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文扩展了正电子素双光子衰变的复合量子场论框架，引入了类比于赝标量介子的弱衰变常数概念，用于量化正电子素场与弱轴向流的耦合，并揭示其在电弱区域的内部结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于正电子素的弱相互作用衰变被强烈抑制，研究其在弱相互作用领域的性质具有挑战性，因此需要发展新的理论工具来描述其复合系统的量子场论特性。

Method: 基于已有的双光子衰变复合QFT框架，引入正电子素的弱衰变常数，并通过类比赝标量介子的方法定义该常数，进而推导出正电子素与其组成粒子之间的顶点函数。

Result: 得到了正电子素弱衰变常数的数值表达式 $ f_{P} \simeq \frac{m_{e}}{2\sqrtπ} α^{3/2} = 89.8593~\mathrm{eV} $，并利用该结果推导出正电子素与其组分之间的顶点函数。

Conclusion: 弱衰变常数为研究正电子素在电弱相互作用下的内部结构提供了新工具，且该方法可推广至其他类似束缚态系统如夸克偶素的研究。

Abstract: The positronium, as the lightest purely leptonic bound state, provides an ideal testing ground for a quantum field--theoretical (QFT) description of composite systems. While its electromagnetic annihilation is well understood as the dominant decay channel, the weak interaction sector of positronium is strongly suppressed. In this work, we extend the composite QFT framework previously developed for the two--photon decay and introduce the concept of a weak decay constant for para--positronium. This constant, defined in analogy with those of pseudoscalar mesons, quantifies the coupling of the positronium field to the weak axial current and serves as a measure of its internal structure in the electroweak domain. Its numerical value $ f_{P} \simeq \frac{m_{e}}{2\sqrtπ} α^{3/2} = 89.8593~\mathrm{eV} $ is, as expected, small. Nevertheless, the resulting expression and a related comparison to quarkonium systems allow us to determine the vertex function linking the positronium to its own constituents.

</details>


### [7] [Improving Neutrino Oscillation Measurements through Event Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11938)
*Sebastian A. R. Ellis,Daniel C. Hackett,Shirley Weishi Li,Pedro A. N. Machado,Karla Tame-Narvaez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种基于机器学习的事件分类方法，在能量重建前按相互作用类型分类，提升中微子能量重建精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有中微子能量重建方法受限于中微子-原子核相互作用模型的不确定性，且未利用不同相互作用通道导致的缺失能量差异这一信息。

Method: 使用监督式机器学习方法，基于生成器标注事件，区分准弹性散射、介子交换电流、共振产生和深度非弹性散射等过程，并在能量重建前进行分类。

Result: 跨生成器测试表明该方法对微观物理模型偏差具有鲁棒性，在DUNE模拟的ν_μ消失分析中提升了能量重建的准确性和测量灵敏度。

Conclusion: 该分类策略为降低未来中微子振荡测量中由重建引起的系统误差提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Precise neutrino energy reconstruction is essential for next-generation long-baseline oscillation experiments, yet current methods remain limited by large uncertainties in neutrino-nucleus interaction modeling. Even so, it is well established that different interaction channels produce systematically varying amounts of missing energy and therefore yield different reconstruction performance--information that standard calorimetric approaches do not exploit. We introduce a strategy that incorporates this structure by classifying events according to their underlying interaction type prior to energy reconstruction. Using supervised machine-learning techniques trained on labeled generator events, we leverage intrinsic kinematic differences among quasi-elastic scattering, meson-exchange current, resonance production, and deep-inelastic scattering processes. A cross-generator testing framework demonstrates that this classification approach is robust to microphysics mismodeling and, when applied to a simulated DUNE $ν_μ$ disappearance analysis, yields improved accuracy and sensitivity. These results highlight a practical path toward reducing reconstruction-driven systematics in future oscillation measurements.

</details>


### [8] [Upper Bound on the Cosmic Baryon Chemical Potential from Lepton-Flavor Asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11995)
*Francesco Di Clemente,Alessandro Drago,Lorenzo Formaggio,Claudia Ratti,Volodymyr Vovchenko,Geetika Yadav*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 研究了在轻子味不对称但总轻子数小的情况下，QCD相变时期的宇宙演化，发现即使存在极端的轻子味不对称，也无法使系统进入一阶相变区域，除非临界点因非零电荷化学势而显著左移，因此限制QCD时期残留物仍处于手征交叉过渡的标准情景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在轻子味不对称情况下QCD相变的宇宙学影响，特别是对早期宇宙中可能的一阶相变或临界行为的约束。

Method: 通过分析不同温度下重子化学势的上限，研究τ-μ和μ-e不对称情形下的宇宙轨迹，并考虑非零电荷化学势对临界点位置的影响。

Result: 发现τ-μ不对称存在局部最大值，μ-e不对称趋近于极限曲线；极端轻子味不对称本身不足以进入一阶相变区，除非临界点大幅左移。

Conclusion: QCD相变时期仍被限制在手征交叉过渡的标准模型框架内，极端轻子味不对称不足以改变这一结论。

Abstract: We study the early Universe trajectory around the QCD transition in lepton-flavor-asymmetric cases with small total lepton asymmetry ($|\ell|\lesssim 10^{-2}$), while allowing large individual lepton asymmetries. For each temperature, we find an upper bound on the baryon chemical potential $μ_{\mathrm B}(T)$: $τ$--$μ$ asymmetric cases exhibit a local maximum, whereas $μ$--$e$ cases approach a limiting curve. Thus, even extreme lepton-flavor asymmetry alone cannot reach a first-order region, unless the critical point is moved to a substantially lower $μ_\mathrm{B}/T$ because of the nonzero $μ_\mathrm{Q}$. Therefore, we constrain the QCD-era relic to the standard scenario of a chiral crossover transition.

</details>


### [9] [Normalization of partial wave CP asymmetries in three-body decays of heavy hadrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12445)
*Jing-Juan Qi,Zhen-Yang Wang,Zhen-Hua Zhang,Xin-Heng Guo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的方法来解决重强子多体衰变中部分波CP不对称性（PWCPA）的归一化问题，通过引入额外因子并使所有PWCPA具有相同统计误差，得到准归一化的结果，并应用于B±→π+π-π±衰变中ρ0(1450)附近的干涉分析，验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 部分波CP不对称性（PWCPA）在多体衰变研究中提供丰富的干涉信息，但存在归一化难题，可能导致误导性结果，因此需要一种可靠的方法来修正这一问题。

Method: 引入一组额外因子对PWCPA进行重缩放，不依据传统归一化条件，而是要求所有PWCPA具有相同的统计误差，从而获得准归一化的PWCPA，并应用于B±→π+π-π±衰变中ρ0(1450)区域的LHCb数据。

Result: 在π+π-不变质量围绕ρ0(1450)的相空间区域，分析了ρ0(1450)、f2(1270)和f0(1500)共振态之间的干涉模式及其对准归一化PWCPA的贡献，结果显示该方法能有效避免其他定义方式可能带来的误导或失真结果。

Conclusion: 所提出的准归一化方法解决了PWCPA的归一化问题，提升了物理结果的可靠性，适用于重强子多体衰变中的CP破坏研究。

Abstract: CP violation in hadronic multi-body decays has been extensively studied, and the experimental breakthrough in the heayy baryon sector was made recently. Partial-Wave CP Asymmetries (PWCPAs) in multi-body decays of heavy hadrons, which although provide us with more interference information, suffer from the normalization problem, as is pointed out in this paper. We propose a novel solution to this problem. We introduce a set of extra factors to rescale the PWCPAs to the proper sizes. Instead of determining the set of factors according to the normalization requirement, we demand that all the PWCPAs have the same statistical errors. In this way, we obtain a set of quasi-normalized PWCPAs, in the sense that they are close to the ideal normalized ones. As an application, we perform an analysis of PWCPAs in the decay channel $B^\pm\toπ^+π^-π^\pm$. We focus on the phase space region where the invariant mass of the $π^+π^-$ pair varies around the vector resonance $ρ^0(1450)$. Based on the data of the LHCb collaboration, the interference patterns among the resonances $ρ^0(1450)$, $f_2(1270)$, and $f_0(1500)$ and their contributions to the quasi-normalized PWCPAs are analyzed. The analysis indicates that the quasi-normalized PWCPAs can avoid potential misleading or distorted results comparing with some other alternatively defined ones.

</details>


### [10] [Vortex states and entanglement properties in multiphoton pair production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12475)
*Hong-Hao Fan,Lie-Juan Li,Zhi-Hang Yao,Orkash Amat,Suo Tang,Bai-Song Xie*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 研究了在圆偏振场中通过双能级模型的多光子对产生，发现动量分布中存在明显的离散环结构，其半径由吸收光子数决定，并受粒子自旋调控。自旋与场旋转方向对齐时环变窄，反平行时变宽，这可通过角动量守恒解释。产生的粒子轨道角动量表现为动量分布相位中的涡旋结构，其拓扑电荷表征该涡旋。还研究了产生粒子间的自旋纠缠，发现纠缠随横向动量增加而增强，并在不同多光子环过渡处（相位涡旋拓扑电荷变化时）出现尖锐峰值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索强场量子电动力学中多光子对产生的机制及其自旋和轨道角动量特性，理解角动量守恒在非微扰区域的作用。

Method: 采用双能级模型研究圆偏振场中的多光子对产生，分析动量分布、相位结构及自旋纠缠特性。

Result: 发现了由吸收光子数决定的离散环状动量分布，揭示了自旋对环宽度的调控作用；观察到相位涡旋结构并关联其拓扑电荷与轨道角动量；发现自旋纠缠随横向动量增强并在多光子环过渡处出现峰值。

Conclusion: 多光子对产生过程中的动量分布、相位涡旋和自旋纠缠均可由角动量守恒解释，自旋-轨道耦合效应显著影响粒子产生特性，为强场QED中的量子调控提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate the multiphoton pair production in circularly polarized field via two level model. There appears obvious discrete ring structures in the momentum distribution of the created particles, in which the ring radius is mainly controlled by the number of the photons absorbed in the creation with the energy conservation and could also be modulated by the spin of the created pair. These multiphoton rings become narrower when both of the pair particles' spin are aligned with the direction of the field rotation, and become broader if both spin are antiparallel to that direction. This spin-modulation can be simply understood with the angular momentum conservation, as less orbital angular momentum from the absorbed photons would be transferred to the created particles if their spins are aligned with the field rotation. The orbital angular momentum of the created particles is manifested as the vortex structure in the phase of the momentum distribution, and valued as the topological charge of this phase vortex. We also study the spin entanglement between the created particles, and reveal that the entanglement becomes stronger with the increase of the particles' transverse momentum, and gets sharp peak in the transition between different multiphoton rings, where the topological charge of the phase vortex is changed.

</details>


### [11] [Tomography of high-twist proton structure through $ep$ elastic scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12589)
*Ji-Xin Yu,Shan Cheng,Jia-Jie Han,Hsiang-nan Li,Fu-Sheng Yu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次基于微扰QCD的kT因子化方法，研究了质子形状因子F1,2(Q^2)的高扭度行为，解释了在中等Q^2区域Q^4F1(Q^2)数据近似标度行为的起源，并提取了直到扭度6的质子LCDA，结果通过Λb→pπ,pK衰变中的电荷共轭不对称性得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于次领头扭度光锥分布振幅（LCDAs）在部分子动量分数端点区域被意外发现有显著增强效应，导致高幂次修正贡献较大，因此需要系统研究这些高扭度效应以理解质子电磁形状因子的行为。

Method: 采用微扰QCD的kT因子化框架，结合kT重求和效应来压制端点发散，分析ep弹性散射中质子形状因子F1,2(Q^2)，并从实验数据中提取直到扭度6的质子LCDAs。

Result: 成功解释了Q^4F1(Q^2)在中等Q^2~O(10) GeV^2区域的近似标度行为；提取出包含端点增强效应的质子LCDAs，并通过Λb→pπ,pK衰变中的电荷-宇称不对称性进行检验，结果一致。

Conclusion: 端点增强效应在kT重求和压制下对描述中等Q^2区质子形状因子至关重要；所提取的高扭度LCDAs为理解质子三维结构提供了新视角，并强调了精确处理强子 exclusive 过程微扰计算的重要性。

Abstract: We present the first high-twist study of the proton form factors $F_{1,2}(Q^2)$ in $ep$ elastic scattering based on the perturbative QCD $k_T$ factorization, $Q^2$ being momentum transfer squared. It is motivated by unexpectedly large higher-power contributions from subleading-twist light-cone distribution amplitudes (LCDAs), which are attributed to the enhancement in endpoint regions of parton momentum fractions. We highlight that the endpoint enhancement, tamed by the $k_T$ resummation effect, is crucial for accommodating the approximate scaling behavior of the $Q^4F_1(Q^2)$ data at intermediate $Q^2\sim {\cal O}(10)$ GeV$^2$. The proton LCDAs up to twist 6 are then extracted, and verified by the charge-parity asymmetries observed in the heavy baryon decays $Λ_b\to pπ, pK$. Our work provides new insights into the proton three-dimensional structure and manifests the precision requirement for reliable perturbative analyses of baryonic exclusive processes.

### [12] [Resurrecting the Standard Model Effective Field Theory interferences at colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12673)
*Matteo Maltoni*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文研究了在标准模型之外可能存在新物理的情况下，利用SMEFT框架中维度-6算符的干涉效应被抑制的现象，并提出了恢复这些干涉的策略，应用于三喷注产生和电弱过程等具体案例，同时引入新的运动学观测量以提高对算符系数的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于当前实验未发现新共振态，但可能存在高能标下的新物理，SMEFT被用于描述对标准模型的小偏差；然而某些情况下维度-6算符与标准模型的干涉被压低，需理解其机制并提出观测策略。

Method: 引入区分不同压制机制（螺旋度不匹配或截面项相消）的物理量，发展恢复干涉现象的方法，并应用于$O_G$和$O_W$算符相关的三喷注、VBF $Zjj$、$WZ$、$Wγ$等过程；最后在一阶匹配部分子 shower 的水平上研究十个四轻夸克算符的多喷注及伴随EW玻色子的过程。

Result: 成功区分了两种干涉压制机制，提出了有效的现象学策略来恢复干涉效应；在多个过程中找到了对压制敏感的简单运动学观测量，可用于获得对算符系数的竞争性限制；对于十个四夸克算符，虽无显著干涉压制，但发现其在NLO可广泛影响多种过程。

Conclusion: 论文提出的工具和方法有助于提升对SMEFT中弱干涉效应的探测能力，即使在SMEFT有效范围之外也能给出有意义的约束，为未来LHC数据分析提供了实用框架。

Abstract: Even if some experimental evidence suggests the existence of physics beyond the SM, no clues of new resonances can be found in the data. In the case their masses are much larger than the energies of current experiments, the SMEFT formalism can be used to introduce new operators that parametrise small deviations from the SM predictions at the LHC, induced by interactions between the known and new states. This thesis focuses on some operators and processes for which the leading correction to the SM, namely its interference with dimension-6 operators, is suppressed, either because it is small all over the phase space as a result of a helicity mismatch in the SM and SMEFT amplitudes, or because a cancellation between large cross-section contributions with opposite sign occurs. Several useful quantities are introduced to distinguish among these two cases, and a phenomenological strategy to revive the interferences is developed. They are applied to the cases of the $O_G$ and $O_W$ operators, respectively in three-jet production and EW processes like VBF $Zjj$, $WZ$ and $Wγ$. The comparison among them highlights how different procedures can be followed to restore the interference. The quantities introduced in this thesis can be used to find simple kinematic observables that are sensitive to the suppression and can yield competitive bounds on the coefficients of the operators, even outside the SMEFT validity region. In the last chapter, a study of ten four-light quark operators is presented at LO matched to parton shower. Individual and marginalised limits on them are obtained through multijet production and processes where the jets are generated together with EW bosons, like $Z, W, γ$+jets. Almost no interference suppression happens for these operators, but they can virtually affect any process at NLO.

In this paper, we resolve this initial conditions problem by proposing a novel modification to gravity based on nonlinear quantum mechanics. We introduce specific state-dependent terms to the Hamiltonian, constructed from expectation values of the metric such as the average Ricci scalar. These terms alter the dynamical equations of gravity such that the shadow energy density associated with unconstrained initial conditions redshifts away with cosmic expansion, rendering it negligible at late times. We demonstrate that this significant infrared modification of gravity is consistent with local and cosmological tests of gravity. We comment on the possibility of testing this solution in cosmological measurements of Newton's constant.

Our calculations yield decay widths for $K^*$ and $ψ(2S)$ that are in excellent agreement with experimental data. For the charm and bottom meson decays, where precise measurements are lacking, we provide theoretical predictions and compare them with other theoretical approaches. Most notably, our analysis reveals a universal linear dependence of the decay width on a function A(x) in the logarithmic coordinate system, which originates from the two-body decay dynamics and the ratio of the initial and final state decay constants. These molecular states are not simple $I = 0$ states, but mixtures of $I = 0$ and $I = 1$ states. Result: 得到了具有同位旋-自旋-宇称IJ^P = 1/2(1/2)^-, 1/2(3/2)^-, 和1/2(5/2)^-的隐粲双奇异五夸克态的质量谱。

Conclusion: 所得到的质量谱可用于指导未来实验搜寻隐粲双奇异五夸克态，特别是在Ξ_b^- → P_{css}^-φ → J/ψΞ^-φ等衰变过程中进行验证。

Abstract: In this work, we construct the color $\bar{\mathbf{3}}\bar{\mathbf{3}}\bar{\mathbf{3}}$ type local five-quark currents with the light quarks $qss$ in the flavor octet, and study the $qssc\bar{c}$ pentaquark states via the QCD sum rules in a comprehensive way. ### [22] [On the Charm Contribution to the Muon $g-2$ Light-by-Light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.13097)

Our final result is $a_μ^{\mathrm{HLbLc}}=3.65(25)\times 10^{-11}$, in good agreement with recent lattice determinations.

### [23] [Roles of $Λ$ resonances in the $K^- p \to γΣ$ reaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.13157)
*Yi Pan,Bo-Chao Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 明确不同 $Λ$ 共振态在 $K^- p \to γΣ$ 反应中的作用，特别是解释实验数据在不同能量区域的行为。

Method: 采用基于有效拉格朗日方法的等离子体模型，包含 s-道超子及其共振、t-道 K 和 K* 交换、u-道质子和 Δ(1232) 交换以及一个唯象接触项。

Result: $Λ(1600)$ 对低能实验数据描述至关重要；在高能区，引入 $Λ(1670)$ 或 $Λ(1690)$ 显著提升与数据的符合度，但当前数据无法区分这两种情况。

Abstract: We investigate the $K^- p \to γΣ$ reaction using an effective Lagrangian approach within an isobar model framework. The model includes contributions from $s$-channel hyperon and hyperon resonance, $t$-channel $K$ and $K^*$, $u$-channel proton and $Δ(1232)$ exchanges, and a phenomenological contact term. Our analysis focuses on the roles of various $Λ$ resonances. The results indicate that the $Λ(1600)$ resonance is crucial for describing the experimental data at lower energies. At higher energies, the inclusion of either the $Λ(1670)$ or the $Λ(1690)$ resonance significantly improves the agreement with data. However, the current data are insufficient to distinguish between these two scenarios. We suggest that future measurements at higher beam energies and the measurement of the $Σ$ polarization are needed to identify the roles of the $Λ(1670)$ and $Λ(1690)$ resonances.

### [24] [Anomalous Higgs Couplings as a Window to New Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.13227)
*I. Asiáin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文研究了有效场论结合幺正化技术在探索超出标准模型物理中的应用，特别是电弱对称性破缺的动力学起源。重点分析了纵向WW散射过程，进行了HEFT框架下的一圈计算，并探讨了横向规范玻色子对动力学共振态质量和宽度的影响。同时，利用幺正性和因果性约束Higgs自相互作用，并将该方法推广到作为有效场论的量子引力理论中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于有效场论在高能下容易破坏幺正性，因此需要幺正化技术来恢复物理可观测性的有效性，特别是在探究电弱对称性破缺机制和Higgs动力学时。

Method: 采用HEFT框架进行全一圈计算，使用on-shell方案确定反项，并结合幺正化与因果性条件分析共振态性质；在标量道中考虑耦合过程以提取Higgs信息；最后将方法应用于量子引力的有效场论。

Result: 发现横向规范玻色子显著影响矢量-同位旋和标量-同位旋通道中动力学共振态的质量与宽度；幺正性和因果性对Higgs自耦合给出了非平庸限制；通过弹性WW散射可间接探测Higgs sector而无需双Higgs产生；该方法可成功应用于量子引力振幅的幺正化。

Conclusion: 有效场论结合幺正化是研究超出标准模型物理的有力工具，尤其适用于难以直接探测的Higgs动力学和标量共振态；该框架为未来高精度电弱测量和新物理搜索提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Throughout this thesis, we investigate how effective field theories, combined with unitarization techniques, can be used to explore physics beyond the Standard Model, with particular emphasis on the dynamical origin of electroweak symmetry breaking. Since effective theories often produce amplitudes that violate unitarity at high energies, restoring unitarity is essential before comparing predictions with data.
  The first part of the work focuses on longitudinal $WW$ scattering, a process that, despite being subdominant at the LHC, provides a sensitive probe of Higgs dynamics. We perform a full one-loop computation within the HEFT framework, determine the required counterterms in the on-shell scheme, and analyze for the first time how the inclusion of transverse gauge bosons modifies the masses and widths of the dynamical resonances obtained through unitarization in the vector--isovector and scalar--isoscalar channels. This provides the technical foundation for studying HEFT low-energy couplings subject to unitarity and causality.
  While vector resonances are relatively well characterized through Weinberg sum rules and unitarization, scalar resonances remain more elusive and depend on HEFT parameters that are experimentally difficult to constrain. We show that unitarization, together with causality, imposes nontrivial bounds on Higgs self-interactions. In the scalar channel, the necessity of treating coupled processes becomes a key ingredient, enabling us to extract information about the Higgs sector from elastic $WW \to WW$ scattering without requiring double-Higgs production.
  Finally, we apply the formalism developed throughout the thesis to unitarize the amplitudes of a quantum theory of gravity treated as an effective field theory, illustrating the broader applicability of these methods.

  <summary>Details</summary>

We extend the SM with a complex singlet scalar (cxSM) and examine the phase transition behavior using a fully general renormalizable scalar potential that permits a complex vacuum expectation value for the singlet and coupled dynamics among multiple scalar fields. ### [27] [$D_{(s)}(2S)$ and $D^{*}_{(s)}(2S)$ production in nonleptonic $B_{(s)}$ weak decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.13456)
*Zhi-Jie Sun,Yong-Jin Sun,Zhi-Qing Zhang,You-Ya Yang,Si-Yang Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文使用协变光前方法研究了B介子到第一径向激发态D(2S)和D*(2S)的非轻子衰变，发现多个衰变道的分支比在10^-5到10^-3之间，可被当前实验探测。理论预测与相对论夸克模型结果一致，且揭示了纵向极化占主导的特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来实验上发现了许多重介子的激发态，包括径向激发态，B介子到这些激发态的衰变过程引起广泛关注。理解这些衰变有助于揭示强相互作用动力学和介子结构。

Method: 采用协变光前（covariant light-front）方法计算B(s)介子到D(s)(2S)和D*(s)(2S)的非轻子衰变过程，并计算分支比和极化性质，同时与BS方程、RQM和RIQM等理论结果进行比较。

Result: 多个衰变道的分支比为10^-5～10^-4，个别可达10^-3；B→D*(2S)相关衰变的分支比高于BS方法预测，但与RQM和RIQM结果吻合；D*(1S)和D*(2S)衰变虽分支比不同，但纵向极化分数均约为90%，表现出相似的极化特性。

Conclusion: B介子到D(2S)和D*(2S)激发态的衰变具有可观测的分支比，适合在当前实验中搜索和测量；理论结果支持使用协变光前方法描述此类过程，且极化行为具有普适性。

Abstract: Recently, many new excited states of heavy mesons have been discovered in recent experiments, including radially excited states. The production processes of these states from the $B_{(s)}$ meson have drawn significant interest. In this paper, we use the covariant light-front approach to study the nonleptonic $B_{(s)}$ meson decays to the first radially excited states $D_{(s)}(2S)$ and $D^{*}_{(s)}(2S)$. Our results reveal that many channels exhibit large branching ratios in the range $10^{-5}\sim 10^{-4}$, even up to $10^{-3}$ for individual channels, which are detectable by current experiments. Our predictions for the decays $B_{(s)}\to D^{(*)}_{(s)}(2S)(π,ρ,K^{(*)})$ are larger than those given by the Bethe-Salpeter (BS) equation method, but agree well with the relativistic quark mode (RQM) and the relativistic independent quark model (RIQM) calculations. For comparison, we also present the branching ratios of the decays $B_{(s)}\to D^{(*)}_{(s)}(1S)(π,ρ,K^{(*)})$, which are comparable with other theoretical results and the data. Although the branching ratios of the decays $B_{(s)} \to D^{*}_{(s)}(1S)(ρ,K^*)$ are much larger than those of the decays $B_{(s)} \to D^{*}_{(s)}(2S)(ρ,K^*)$, the polarization properties between them are similar, that is, the longitudinal polarization fractions are dominant and can amount roughly to $90\%$.

On- and off-shell production of such scalar particles leads to characteristic distortions in the double beta decay electron spectrum. We investigate how these distortions would manifest in current and future double beta decay experiments, deriving the sensitivity to such scenarios. We project the reach of future experiments which can probe scalar-neutrino couplings of $|a_ν| \approx 2\times 10^{-6}$ for sub-MeV scalar particles and remain sensitive to off-shell production above the Q-value of double beta decay isotopes.

We show that the large set of clean observables available at lepton colliders is more that sufficient to resolve any of these ambiguities. Motivation: 标准的钱德拉塞卡动力学摩擦公式在具有恒定密度核心的系统中失效，无法解释核心停滞和动力学浮力现象，因此需要从相空间分布函数的角度系统研究这些效应的物理起源。

Method: 采用高分辨率N体模拟结合动理学理论分析，研究不同密度轮廓下宿主系统的分布函数特征及其对动力学摩擦方向和效率的影响。

Result: 发现核心停滞发生在扰动物遇到分布函数平台区时，而浮力则源于分布函数的拐点引发的不稳定偶极模式；双幂律密度轮廓在过渡陡峭时易产生此类特征，导致相似结构核心出现截然不同的动力学结果。

Conclusion: 提出了一个统一框架，将星系的相空间结构与嵌入大质量天体的命运联系起来，对矮星系和椭圆星系中的黑洞并合停滞、活动星系核偏心及核星团动力学等有直接意义。

Abstract: Dynamical friction governs the orbital decay of massive perturbers within galaxies and dark matter halos, yet its standard Chandrasekhar formulation fails in systems with cores of (roughly) constant density, where inspiral can halt or even reverse, phenomena known respectively as core stalling and dynamical buoyancy. Although these effects have been observed in simulations, the conditions under which they arise remain unclear. Using high-resolution N-body simulations and analytic insights from kinetic theory, we systematically explore the physical origin of these effects. We demonstrate that the overall distribution function (DF) of the host, not just its central density gradient, determines the efficiency and direction of dynamical friction. Core stalling arises when the perturber encounters a plateau in the DF, either pre-existing or dynamically created through its own inspiral, while buoyancy emerges in systems whose DFs possess an inflection that drives an unstable dipole mode. We show that double power-law density profiles with rapid outer-to-inner slope transitions naturally produce such DF features, which is why structurally similar cores can yield radically different dynamical outcomes. Our results provide a unified framework linking the phase-space structure of galaxies to the fate of embedded massive objects, with direct implications for off-center AGN, the dynamics of nuclear star clusters, and the stalled coalescence of black holes in dwarf galaxies and massive ellipticals.

</details>


### [32] [LEGA-C stellar populations scaling relations. II: Dissecting mass-complete archaeological trends and their evolution since z~0.7 with LEGA-C and SDSS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11805)
*Anna R. Gallazzi,Stefano Zibetti,Arjen van der Wel,Angelos Nersesian,Yasha Kaushal,Rachel Bezanson,Daniele Mattolini,Eric F. Bell,Laura Scholz-Diaz,Joel Leja,Francesco D'Eugenio,Po-Feng Wu,Camilla Pacifici,Michael Maseda*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究利用LEGA-C巡天中552个红移约0.7的星系，探讨恒星形成对恒星年龄和金属丰度的影响，并分析其与恒星质量或速度弥散的关系。发现恒星年龄-质量关系存在双峰分布，源于宁静与恒星形成星系的不同年龄分布；而金属丰度-质量关系无明显双峰，但在低质量区斜率变陡。与本地样本对比显示，低质量恒星形成星系自z~0.7以来显著富集，且中位年龄演化小于宇宙年龄增长，需结合个体与群体演化机制解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解星系在红移z~0.7时的恒星年龄和金属丰度与其恒星形成活动的关系，揭示星系演化过程中质量、金属丰度和恒星形成历史的关联，并量化从z~0.7到现在的演化趋势。

Method: 使用LEGA-C巡天中552个z~0.7星系的光谱数据，结合SDSS DR7光谱进行一致性分析，并考虑孔径改正，研究恒星年龄和金属丰度与恒星质量或速度弥散的关系，并比较高红移与本地星系的中位趋势演化。

Result: 恒星年龄-质量关系呈现双峰分布，源于宁静与恒星形成星系的不同年龄分布；金属丰度-质量关系无双峰，但两类星系分布不同，且低质量恒星形成星系金属丰度弥散增大；z~0.7到z=0.1期间，宁静星系金属丰度几乎未演化，低质量恒星形成星系金属丰度显著增加，中位年龄变化仅约2 Gyr，小于宇宙老化预期。

Conclusion: 星系的恒星年龄和金属丰度演化受恒星形成状态影响显著；低质量星系自z~0.7以来经历了明显的化学演化；仅靠被动演化不足以解释观测到的中位趋势变化，需引入再激活、微并合及大质量富金属星系的淬火等过程共同作用。

Abstract: With a sample of 552 galaxies at z~0.7 from the LEGA-C survey, we investigate how current star formation influences light-weighted mean stellar ages and metallicities, and their median trends with stellar mass or velocity dispersion. The bimodality in the global age-mass relation stems from the different age distributions in the quiescent (Q) and star-forming (SF) populations. A bimodality is not observed in the stellar metallicity-mass relation, although Q and SF galaxies have different distributions in this parameter space. We identify a high-metallicity sequence populated by both Q and weakly SF galaxies. At masses below logM/Msun=10.8 the median stellar metallicity-mass relation of SF galaxies steepens, as a consequence of increasing scatter toward lower stellar metallicities for galaxies with increasing specific star formation rate at fixed mass. With a consistent analysis of SDSS DR7 spectra, accounting for aperture corrections, we quantify the evolution of the stellar age and stellar metallicity scaling relations between z=0.7 and the present. We find negligible evolution in the stellar metallicity-mass relation of Q galaxies and for logM/Msun>11 galaxies in general. Lower mass SF galaxies, instead, have typically lower metallicities than their local counterparts, indicating significant enrichment since z~0.7 in the low-mass regime. The median of the stellar ages of both the general population and Q galaxies has changed by only 2 Gyr between z=0.7 and z=0.1, less than expected from cosmic aging. Some Q galaxies must evolve passively to reach the old boundary of the local population. However, in order to explain the evolution of the median trends, both individual evolution, through rejuvenation and/or minor merging impacting the outer galaxy regions, and population evolution, through quenching of massive, metal-rich star-forming galaxies, are required. (Abridged)

### [33] [ODIN: Characterizing the Three-dimensional Structure of Two Protocluster Complexes at $z = 3.1$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11826)
*Vandana Ramakrishnan,Ashley Ortiz,Byeongha Moon,Eunsoo Jun,David Schlegel,Kyoung-Soo Lee,Jessica Nicole Aguilar,Maria Celeste Artale,David Brooks,Maria Candela Cerdosino,Robin Ciardullo,Todd Claybaugh,Andrei Cuceu,Axel de la Macorra,Arjun Dey,Nicole M. Firestone,Andreu Font-Ribera,Jaime E. Forero-Romero,Eric Gawiser,Enrique Gaztañaga,Caryl Gronwall,Lucia Guaita,Gaston Gutierrez,Sungryong Hong,Ho Seong Hwang,Sang Hyeok Im,Paulina Troncoso Iribarren,Woong-Seob Jeong,Dick Joyce,Ankit Kumar,Claire Lamman,Martin Landriau,Seong-Kook Lee,Jaehyun Lee,Aaron Meisner,Ramon Miquel,John Moustakas,Seshadri Nadathur,Gautam Nagaraj,Julie Nantais,Nelson Padilla,Changbom Park,Will Percival,Francisco Prada,Ignasi Pérez-Ràfols,Graziano Rossi,Eusebio Sanchez,Joseph Harry Silber,Hyunmi Song,David Sprayberry,Gregory Tarlé,Francisco Valdes,Yujin Yang,Ann Zabludoff,Hu Zou*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用ODIN巡天数据和多台望远镜的光谱后随观测，对红移z=3.1处的两个原星系团复合体COSMOS-z3.1-A和COSMOS-z3.1-C的三维形态进行了详细分析，揭示了其不规则且沿单一轴线延伸的结构，并发现多个密度峰及可能的宇宙纤维结构，证实COSMOS-z3.1-A为早期宇宙中的原超星系团，未来将演化成质量超过Coma星系团的超大质量结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高红移宇宙中大规模结构的形成与演化，特别是原星系团和原超星系团的三维形态及其环境特征，对于揭示星系形成和宇宙大尺度结构的组装过程至关重要。

Method: 结合ODIN巡天中测光选出的莱曼-alpha发射体（LAEs）与Keck、Gemini和DESI的光谱确认样本，采用概率性方法重建z=3.1处原星系团复合体在约50 cMpc尺度上的三维结构，并利用IllustrisTNG300-1模拟验证重建方法的有效性。

Result: 三维重构显示两个复合体均呈不规则且沿单轴拉长，包含多个密度峰（A中有10个，C中有4个），并观察到连接核心的‘尾状’结构，可能代表向高密度区供能的宇宙纤维；Lyα斑块倾向于分布在最高密度区域的外围；质量估计表明这两个结构在z=0时总质量将超过log(M/M☉) ≳ 15.3，比Coma星系团更庞大。

Conclusion: COSMOS-z3.1-A是迄今在更早宇宙时期观测到的类似Hyperion的原超星系团，其复杂结构突显了视线方向对结构形态认知的影响，研究支持星系团通过宇宙纤维从周围环境吸积物质逐步形成的理论。

Abstract: We present a detailed study of the 3D morphology of two extended associations of multiple protoclusters at $z=3.1$. These protocluster `complexes', designated COSMOS-z3.1-A and COSMOS-z3.1-C, are the most prominent overdensities of $z=3.1$ Ly$α$ emitters (LAEs) identified in the COSMOS field by the One-hundred-deg$^2$ DECam Imaging in Narrowbands (ODIN) survey. These protocluster complexes have been followed up with extensive spectroscopy from Keck, Gemini, and DESI. Using a probabilistic method that combines photometrically selected and spectroscopically confirmed LAEs, we reconstruct the 3D structure of these complexes on scales of $\approx$50 cMpc. We validate our reconstruction method using the IllustrisTNG300-1 cosmological hydrodynamical simulation and show that it consistently outperforms approaches relying solely on spectroscopic data. The resulting 3D maps reveal that both complexes are irregular and elongated along a single axis, emphasizing the impact of sightline on our perception of structure morphology. The complexes consist of multiple density peaks, ten in COSMOS-z3.1-A and four in COSMOS-z3.1-C. The former is confirmed to be a proto-supercluster, similar to {\it Hyperion} at $z=2.4$ but observed at an even earlier epoch. Multiple `tails' connected to the cores of the density peaks are seen, likely representing cosmic filaments feeding into these extremely overdense regions. The 3D reconstructions further provide strong evidence that Ly$α$ blobs preferentially reside in the outskirts of the highest density regions. Descendant mass estimates of the density peaks suggest that COSMOS-z3.1-A and COSMOS-z3.1-C will evolve to become ultra-massive structures by $z=0$, with total masses $\log(M/M_\odot) \gtrsim 15.3$, exceeding that of Coma.

### [34] [Infrared Signatures of Dusty Tori Formed by MHD-Driven Outflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11835)
*Ruiyu Pan,Arkaprabha Sarangi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究通过构建复杂的三维辐射转移模型，结合Spitzer太空望远镜的中红外光谱数据，探究活动星系核（AGN）中心区域的物理结构与环境。研究比较了两种尘埃密度分布（$r^{-2}$ 和 $r^{-1}$），发现$r^{-1}$分布能更优地拟合观测光谱，支持磁流体动力学（MHD）模型的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示AGN中心区域尘埃环的物理结构和条件，检验不同理论模型（如辐射压驱动风与MHD模型）对尘埃分布的预测能力。

Method: 构建基于物理机制的三维辐射转移模型，包含完整的尘埃颗粒模型，并对Spitzer IRS的20个观测光谱进行拟合，比较$r^{-2}$和$r^{-1}$两种尘埃密度分布的拟合优度（$χ^2$）。

Result: 模型成功再现了从低倾角的9.7μm发射到高倾角吸收的转变现象；在20个样本中，有18个显示$r^{-1}$密度分布的拟合显著优于$r^{-2}$分布。

Conclusion: 研究结果验证了所建模型的物理一致性，并为AGN尘埃环遵循$r^{-1}$密度分布提供了有力证据，支持MHD模型对尘埃环结构的预测。

Abstract: We aim to probe the physical structure and conditions of the central regions of active galactic nuclei (AGN) by interpreting their mid-infrared observational spectra. We constructed a sophisticated three-dimensional radiative transfer model of the AGN source and dusty torus, built upon a physically motivated framework that includes a comprehensive dust grain model. To investigate the properties of the circumnuclear medium, we performed model fitting to a sample of 20 observational spectra from Spitzer Space Telescope's IRS Enhanced Data Products, testing two distinct dust density laws: a steep $r^{-2}$ profile, characteristic of a radiation pressure-driven wind, and a shallower $r^{-1}$ profile, which is a key prediction of magnetohydrodynamic (MHD) models. Our model successfully reproduces fundamental observational phenomena, such as the transition from 9.7\,$μ$m silicate emission at low inclinations to deep absorption at high inclinations, with absorption features becoming more pronounced for higher accretion rates, dust-to-gas ratios, and black hole masses. Most importantly, a direct comparison of the fitting results revealed that the $r^{-1}$ density law provided a significantly better fit ($χ^2$) than the $r^{-2}$ density law for 18 of the 20 observational spectra. These results confirm the physical consistency of our advanced radiative model and provide compelling evidence that an $r^{-1}$ density law is a more accurate representation of the AGN dusty torus.

### [35] [PAH Marks the Spot: Digging for Buried Clusters in Nearby Star-forming Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11920)
*Gabrielle B. Graham,Daniel A. Dale,Chase L. Smith,Elisabeth Brann,Kaycee D. Conder,Samuel Crowe,Sumitra Dhileepkumar,Nicole A. Imming,Emilio Mendez,Zachary Pleska,Kelsey Sako,Amirnezam Amiri,Ashley T. Barnes,Médéric Boquien,Rupali Chandar,Ryan Chown,Oleg Y. TL;DR: 本研究利用哈勃太空望远镜（HST）和詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（JWST）的多波段数据，结合公民科学平台Zooniverse，对11个近邻恒星形成星系中的292个嵌入式年轻星团候选体进行了识别与分析，并通过恒星群体模型确定其年龄、质量及消光特性；研究还基于该样本训练了多种卷积神经网络模型，探索了深度迁移学习在星团搜寻中的应用潜力，为未来更大样本的星团自动识别提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在利用HST和JWST的强大红外观测能力，系统性地识别和表征附近星系中被尘埃遮蔽的年轻星团，克服传统光学波段观测的局限，并推动自动化识别方法的发展。

Method: 结合PHANGS-JWST与PHANGS-HST数据，在近紫外/光学/近红外波段以及Paschenα、Hα发射线和3.3μm PAH特征上进行目视搜索，利用Zooniverse平台识别嵌入式星团候选体；通过恒星群体模型拟合测光数据获得年龄、质量和消光；并使用这些样本训练多个卷积神经网络进行迁移学习，比较不同模型配置的性能。

Result: 共识别出292个嵌入式星团候选体，中位年龄为4.5百万年，平均视线方向消光<AV>=6.0 mag，恒星质量下限中位数为10^3太阳质量；构建了八个不同配置的CNN模型，评估其混淆矩阵与识别趋势，发现经过训练样本优化后的模型具备推广至更大星系样本的潜力。

Conclusion: 结合人机协同的目视识别与深度学习方法可有效构建高质量训练集，并实现嵌入式星团的高效自动识别，为未来大规模星系巡天中的星团普查提供了可靠的技术路径。

Abstract: The joint capabilities of the Hubble Space Telescope (HST) and JWST allow for an unparalleled look at the early lives of star clusters at near- and mid-infrared wavelengths. We present here a multiband analysis of embedded young stellar clusters in 11 nearby, star-forming galaxies, using the PHANGS-JWST and PHANGS-HST datasets. We use the Zooniverse citizen science platform to conduct an initial by-eye search for embedded clusters in near-UV/optical/near-infrared images that trace stellar continuum emission, the Paschen$α$ and H$α$ recombination lines, and the 3.3 $μ$m polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbon feature and its underlying continuum. With this approach, we identify 292 embedded cluster candidates for which we characterize their ages, masses, and levels of line-of-sight extinction by comparing the photometric data to predictions from stellar population models. The embedded cluster candidates have a median age of 4.5 Myr and an average line-of-sight extinction $\left< A_V \right> = 6.0$ mag. We determine lower limits on source stellar masses, resulting in a median stellar mass of $10^3$ $M_{\odot}$. We use this sample of embedded cluster candidates to train multiple convolutional neural network models to carry out deep transfer learning-based searches for embedded clusters. With the aim of optimizing models for future catalog production, we compare results for four variations of training data using two neural networks. Confusion matrices for all eight model configurations, as well as inter-model identification trends, are presented. With refinement of the training sample, we determine that optimized models could serve as a pathway for future embedded cluster identification beyond our 11 galaxy sample.

Magliocchetti,F. Mannucci,C. J. A. P. Martins,L. Maurin,M. Miluzio,P. Monaco,C. Moretti,G. Morgante,K. Naidoo,A. Navarro-Alsina,S. Nesseris,D. Paoletti,F. Passalacqua,K. Paterson,L. Patrizii,A. Pisani,D. Potter,S. Quai,M. Radovich,S. Sacquegna,M. Sahlén,E. Sarpa,A. Schneider,D. Sciotti,E. Sellentin,L. C. Smith,K. Tanidis,C. Tao,G. Testera,R. Teyssier,S. Tosi,A. Troja,M. Tucci,A. Venhola,D. Vergani,G. Verza,P. Vielzeuf,N. A. Walton*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用Euclid Q1数据和其他多波段观测，在z=5-7范围内探测到145个质量大于10^10.25太阳质量的高红移星系，表面密度约为6.3 deg^-2，为当前模型提供了与标准恒星形成效率一致的支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验星系形成模型在高红移时期大质量星系的存在与性质预测。

Method: 结合Euclid、Spitzer IRAC及地面光学数据进行SED拟合，通过严格筛选识别z=5-7且M* > 10^10.25 Msun的大质量星系候选体。

Result: 发现145个候选大质量星系，其中5个M* > 10^11 Msun；半数星系年龄接近宇宙年龄，表明早期形成；78%位于主序星形成区，12%为星暴星系，存在显著尘埃消光（E(B-V)高达0.75）。

Conclusion: 观测结果与标准恒星形成效率下的星系形成模型一致，未发现AGN污染导致高sSFR的显著证据，支持早期宇宙中已有大质量星系形成。

Abstract: Probing the presence and properties of massive galaxies at high redshift is one of the most critical tests for galaxy formation models. In this work, we search for galaxies with stellar masses M* > 10^10.25 Msun at z in [5,7], i.e., towards the end of the Epoch of Reionisation, over a total of ~23 deg^2 in two of the Euclid Quick Data Release (Q1) fields: the Euclid Deep Field North and Fornax (EDF-N and EDF-F). In addition to the Euclid photometry, we incorporate Spitzer Infrared Camera (IRAC) and ground-based optical data to perform spectral energy distribution (SED) fitting, obtaining photometric redshifts and derived physical parameters. After applying rigorous selection criteria, we identify a conservative sample of 145 candidate massive galaxies with M* > 10^10.25 Msun at z in [5,7], including 5 objects with M* > 10^11 Msun. This makes for a surface density of about 6.3 deg^-2 at z in [5,7], which should be considered a lower limit because of the current depth of the Euclid data (H_E < 24, 5 sigma in Q1). We find that the inferred stellar masses are consistent with galaxy formation models with standard star-formation efficiencies. These massive galaxies have colour excess E(B-V) values up to 0.75, indicating significant dust attenuation in some of them. In addition, half of the massive galaxies have best-fit ages comparable to the age of the Universe at those redshifts, which suggests that their progenitors were formed very early in cosmic time. About 78% of the massive galaxies lie on the star-forming main sequence (MS) in the SFR-M* plane, ~12% are found in the starburst region, and 10% in the transition zone between the MS and starbursts. We find no significant evidence for outshining or AGN contamination that could account for the elevated specific star-formation rates (sSFR) observed in the ~12% of galaxies classified as starbursts.

### [37] [Formation of Close Binaries through Massive Black Hole Perturbations and Chaotic Tides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11965)
*Howard Hao-Tse Huang,Wenbin Lu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的物理模型，考虑了超大质量黑洞（MBH）与双星系统之间的轨道松弛、潮汐扰动及恒星间的动力学潮汐作用。研究表明，在多次近心点通过时，MBH的重复潮汐扰动可使双星内轨道达到极高偏心率，导致恒星振荡模式混沌增长并迅速硬化双星系统至半长轴小于等于10倍恒星半径。高达50%原本宽分离的双星不会直接经历Hills分裂，而是先经历潮汐硬化成为紧密双星，这为产生最快速的超高速星提供了新通道，并与重复部分潮汐瓦解事件和准周期爆发等核瞬变现象相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解超大质量黑洞如何影响双星系统的演化，特别是探索除了传统Hills机制外是否还有其他途径可以生成超高速星以及相关的天文瞬变现象。

Method: 建立一个包含外轨道松弛、MBH潮汐扰动以及双星内部动力学潮汐相互作用的物理模型，并分析这些因素对双星系统长期演化的综合影响。

Result: 发现当双星内轨道达到高偏心率时，恒星振荡模式会混沌增长，快速硬化双星至半长轴a_b≲10R_*；最多50%初始较宽的双星不会直接发生Hills breakup，而是先经历潮汐硬化过程。

Conclusion: 潮汐硬化双星提供了一个新的渠道来生成最快的超高速星，并且与一些核区瞬变现象如重复部分潮汐破坏事件和准周期爆发有关。

Abstract: Hills breakup of binary systems allows massive black holes (MBH) to produce hyper-velocity stars (HVSs) and tightly bound stars. The long timescale of orbital relaxation means that binaries must spend numerous orbits around the MBH before they are tidally broken apart. Repeated MBH tidal perturbations over multiple pericenter passages can perturb the binary inner orbit to high eccentricities, leading to strong tidal interactions between the stars. In this work, we develop a physical model of the MBH-binary system, taking into account outer orbital relaxation, MBH tidal perturbations, and tidal interactions between the binaries in the form of dynamical tides. We show that when the inner orbit reaches high eccentricities such that the pericenter radius is only a few times stellar radii ($R_*$), the stellar oscillation modes can grow chaotically and rapidly harden the binaries to semi-major axes $a_b\lesssim 10\,R_*$. We find that a significant fraction (up to 50\%) of initially wide binaries that are in the empty loss-cone regime ($a_b\sim 1.0\,{\rm AU}$) do not undergo Hills breakup as wide binaries, but instead experience chaotic growth of tides and become close binaries. These tidally hardened binaries provide a new channel for the production of the fastest HVSs, and are connected to other nuclear transients such as repeating partial tidal disruption events and quasi-periodic eruptions.

</details>


### [38] [First Light And Reionisation Epoch Simulations (FLARES) XX: Comparing semi-analytic models at high-redshift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11982)
*Louise T. C. Seeyave,Carlton M. Baugh,Angel Chandro-Gomez,Claudia del P. Lagos,Robert M. Yates,L. Y. Aaron Yung,Rachel S. Somerville,Stephen M. Wilkins,Christopher C. Lovell,William J. Roper,Aswin P. Vijayan,Cedric G. Lacey,Chris Power,Shihong Liao,Maxwell G. A. Maltz,Jack C. Turner*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了不同星系形成模型对高红移星系性质预测的影响，使用FLARES方法比较了EAGLE流体动力学模型和多个半解析模型（SAMs），发现它们在恒星质量函数上较为一致，但在超大质量黑洞性质和被动星系的淬灭机制上存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨不同星系形成模型在高红移环境下预测结果的差异，以理解模型假设对星系演化预测的影响。

Method: 采用FLARES zoom重模拟策略，在红移5到12范围内比较EAGLE模型与GALFORM、L-Galaxies、SC-SAM和SHARK等半解析模型的预测结果，分析恒星质量函数、恒星-晕质量关系、恒星形成率及超大质量黑洞特性。

Result: 各模型预测的恒星质量函数与观测基本一致；但在超大质量黑洞质量上差异显著，GALFORM和SHARK预测的黑洞比L-Galaxies和SC-SAM重1.5–3 dex；在被动星系方面，L-Galaxies和SC-SAM主要依赖环境淬灭，而GALFORM和SHARK中约40%由AGN反馈淬灭，EAGLE模型则显示AGN反馈对中心和卫星星系均至关重要。

Conclusion: 不同星系形成模型在高红移星系演化关键物理过程（如AGN反馈和淬灭机制）上的处理方式显著影响其预测结果，需结合多模型比较以更全面理解星系演化。

Abstract: We explore how the choice of galaxy formation model affects the predicted properties of high-redshift galaxies. Using the FLARES zoom resimulation strategy, we compare the EAGLE hydrodynamics model and the GALFORM, L-Galaxies, SC-SAM and SHARK semi-analytic models (SAMs) at $5\leq z \leq 12$. The first part of our analysis examines the stellar mass functions, stellar-to-halo mass relations, star formation rates, and supermassive black hole (SMBH) properties predicted by the different models. Comparisons are made with observations, where relevant. We find general agreement between the range of predicted and observed stellar mass functions. The model predictions differ considerably when it comes to SMBH properties, with GALFORM and SHARK predicting between 1.5-3 dex more massive SMBHs ($M_{\rm BH}>10^6\ {\rm M_\odot}$) than L-Galaxies and SC-SAM, depending on redshift. The second half of our analysis focuses on passive galaxies. We show that in L-Galaxies and SC-SAM, environmental quenching of satellites is the prevalent quenching mechanism, with active galactic nuclei (AGN) feedback having little effect at the redshifts probed. On the other hand, $\sim40\%$ of passive galaxies predicted by GALFORM and SHARK are quenched by AGN feedback at $z=5$. The SAMs are an interesting contrast to the EAGLE model, in which AGN feedback is essential for the formation of passive galaxies, in both satellites and centrals, even at high redshift.

### [39] [The Impact of Orbital Anisotropy Assumptions in Lensing-Dynamics Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12013)
*Yan Liang,Dandan Xu,Anowar J. Shajib,Yiping Shu,Ran Li*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 研究了在联合引力透镜和恒星动力学建模中，由于假设恒星轨道各向异性可能引入的系统性偏差。使用TNG100模拟中的大质量早期型星系生成自洽的模拟数据集，结果表明常见的各向异性假设（如各向同性、恒定各向异性或Osipkov-Merritt剖面）在星系质量密度分布推断中不会引入显著的系统性偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨在联合引力透镜与恒星动力学建模中，对恒星轨道各向异性的常见假设是否会导致系统性偏差，从而影响星系质量分布的准确推断。

Method: 利用TNG100模拟中红移z=0.2, 0.5, 0.7的早期型星系，构建包含引力透镜和恒星运动学观测的自洽模拟数据集；通过考虑暗物质与重子物质共同作用的势能及用logistic函数描述的径向各向异性变化，结合透镜和动力学约束分离恒星与暗物质贡献，并测试三种常见各向异性假设下的模型推断结果。

Result: 在三种常见各向异性假设下，总恒星质量平均低估小于0.03±0.10 dex，中心暗物质分数仅增加不足2%±10%，偏差不显著；但暗物质内密度斜率被高估0.15±0.2。这些偏差对真实轨道各向异性与模型假设之间的差异不敏感。

Conclusion: 常用的恒星轨道各向异性假设在群体水平上不会对星系质量密度分布的推断引入显著系统性偏差，支持其在实际观测分析中的可靠性。

Abstract: We investigate potential systematic biases introduced by assumptions regarding stellar orbital anisotropy in joint lensing-dynamics modeling. Our study employs the massive early-type galaxies from the TNG100 simulation at redshifts z = 0.2, 0.5, and 0.7. Based on the simulated galaxies, we generate a self-consistent mock dataset containing both lensing and stellar kinematic observables. This is achieved through taking the potential composed of both dark matter and baryons of the simulated galaxies, plus the radial variation of the stellar orbit anisotropy depicted by a logistic function. By integrating constraints from both lensing and stellar kinematics, we separate the contributions of stars and dark matter inside the galaxies. Under three commonly adopted stellar anisotropy assumptions (isotropic orbits, constant anisotropy, and the Osipkov-Merritt profile), the model inferences suggest that the systematic biases in the total stellar mass and central dark matter fraction are not significant. Specifically, the total stellar mass on average is underestimated by less than $0.03\pm0.10$ $\rm dex$ while the dark matter fraction experiences only a statistically insignificant increase of less than $2\%\pm10\%$ at the population level. The dark matter inner density slope in our tests is over-predicted by $0.15\pm0.2$. Additionally, these lacks of significant biases are insensitive to the discrepancies between the assumed anisotropy in modeling and the ground truth orbital anisotropy of mock sample. Our results suggest that conventional assumptions regarding orbital anisotropy, such as an isotropic profile or the Osipkov-Merritt model, would not introduce a significant systematic bias when inferring galaxy mass density distribution at the population level.

</details>


### [40] [Dual core system candidates: a sample of objects with large velocity offset between absorption and narrow emission lines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12021)
*Zheng Qi,Zhang Xueguang,Yuan Qirong*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究从SDSS DR16数据中识别出28个具有显著窄Hβ和Hα发射线速度偏移（>200 km/s）的低红移星系，分析其光谱特征和成像性质，发现多数为双核系统候选体，支持双活动星系核的存在，并对黑洞并合演化提供观测依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找具有大速度偏移的窄发射线天体，探究其动力学起源（如旋转盘、外流或双核系统），并识别可能的超大质量黑洞并合前身系统。

Method: 利用SDSS DR16光谱数据，通过Baldwin-Phillips-Terlevich图进行分类，测量窄线与吸收线之间的速度偏移、线宽及不对称性，并结合测光图像检查双核或并合特征。

Result: 样本呈现不对称的速度偏移分布（17个红移，11个蓝移），窄Hβ偏移与偏度无显著相关性，不支持单纯旋转盘模型；红移系统中窄Hα偏移与线宽呈弱反相关，不符外出流模型；多个目标显示双核或并合图像特征，窄线速度偏移一致性支持双核解释。

Conclusion: 这些具有大速度偏移的天体很可能是双核系统（如并合中的星系或双AGN），可用于未来搜寻高红移宇宙中正在并合的超大质量黑洞对，约束其形成与演化路径。

Abstract: We present a sample of 28 objects at z<0.3 from Data Release 16 of the Sloan Digital Sky Survey (SDSS DR16) with large velocity offset (> 200 km/s) of narrow H$β$ and H$α$ emission lines relative to absorption lines. Diagnostic classification via the Baldwin-Phillips-Terlevich diagram indicates that the sample comprises 12 AGNs, 12 composite galaxies, 3 H{\sc ii} galaxies, and 1 object of uncertain classification. A strong correlation is found between stellar mass and velocity dispersion. We examine the asymmetries of the narrow H$β$ and find that the correlation between velocity offset and narrow H$β$ skewness is negligible in both blue-shifted and red-shifted systems, suggesting that the rotating disk model may not fully explain the observed kinematics. The sample exhibits an asymmetric velocity offset distribution, with more red-shifted (17) than blue-shifted (11) objects. No significant correlation is observed between velocity offset and line width in blue-shifted systems, while red-shifted systems show a weak anti-correlation for narrow H$α$, which is inconsistent with the outflow model. The similarity in velocity offset between narrow emission lines supports the dual core system. Furthermore, the SDSS photometric images reveal eight objects with two cores and two with merger features. Based on the narrow emission line properties, the objects in our sample represent strong candidates for dual core systems exhibiting velocity offset. Extending this property to higher-redshift populations in the near future may facilitate the identification of merging supermassive black hole pairs at earlier cosmic epochs, providing critical constraints on their formation and evolution.

### [41] [3D extinction maps of the Milky Way disc from Gaia GSP-Spec parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12156)
*M. Barbillon,A. Recio-Blanco,P. de Laverny,P. A. Palicio*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用Gaia DR3中560万颗恒星的光谱化学物理参数，提出了一种高均匀性的方法来估算Gaia BP/RP波段的消光，构建了太阳附近高分辨率的三维星际尘埃分布图，并揭示了尘埃、气体和恒星在银河系旋臂结构中的空间关联及其对化学和动力学演化的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了理解银河系星际介质的结构，并校正受尘埃影响的天体物理观测，需要精确的三维星际尘埃分布图。现有消光估计方法常受消光本身影响，本文旨在提供更准确、不受消光偏差影响的新消光估算方法，并探索尘埃与银河旋臂等结构的空间关系。

Method: 基于Gaia GSP-Spec提供的560万颗恒星的大气参数（Teff、log(g)、[M/H]），这些参数独立于消光估计；通过将观测到的(BP-RP)颜色与理论颜色对比计算消光；采用球坐标离散化方法构建三维差分消光图：大尺度图覆盖4x4x0.8 kpc（分辨率40 pc, 1°, 1°），小尺度图聚焦本地泡区域1x1x0.8 kpc（分辨率30 pc, 1°, 1°）。

Result: 成功生成了高分辨率的三维消光地图，显示尘埃分布与分子云及银河旋臂高度相关；在本地泡及更大尺度上识别出多个与气体密度、年轻恒星分布和化学丰度模式一致的结构；证明了尘埃分布与其他星际介质成分的空间一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了基于Gaia数据的新型高精度三维消光图，揭示了星际尘埃、气体和恒星在银河系旋臂中的协同分布，支持了旋臂作为星际介质化学与动力学演化关键框架的观点，为未来银河系结构和演化研究提供了重要工具和视角。

Abstract: 3D maps of interstellar dust are crucial for understanding the structure of the Milky Way interstellar medium to apply correction to astrophysical observations affected by dust. We aim at providing new extinction estimates in the Gaia BP/RP bands to study the dust distribution in the disc, to provide new views of the spatial distribution of extinction and to compare it with tracers of the Galactic spiral arms. We use a highly homogeneous method based on the spectral chemo-physical parametrisation of stars from Gaia General Stellar Parametriser-Spectroscopy (GSP-Spec). This catalogue of 5.6 million stars in DR3, presents the advantage of estimating the stellar atmospheric parameters independently of extinction. The extinction is calculated by comparing the observed stellar (BP-RP) colours in the Gaia bands with the theoretical ones assuming a theoretical Teff-log(g)-[M/H] relation, from the GSP-Spec parameters. Publicly available, 3D high-resolution maps around the Sun are produced through the computation of differential extinction by discretising the dataset into spherical coordinates. Our large scale map covers a region of 4x4x0.8 kpc centred on the Sun with a discretisation of (dr,dθ,dφ)=(40pc,1°,1°). To exploit the higher number of stars in the Sun proximity, we created a smaller scale map focused on the Local Bubble area, with a volume of 1x1x0.8 kpc and a finer discretisation of (dr,dθ,dφ)=(30pc,1°,1°). The produced extinction maps exhibit a strong spatial correlation with molecular clouds and the spiral arms. Interestingly, several regions of the map are consistently present in different tracers as density of gas, of young stars and the chemical pattern of the spiral arms. Our study unveils the link between the distribution of dust, gas, and stars governing the chemical and dynamical evolution of the spiral arms in the Galactic framework.

### [42] [Chemically primitive dwarf accretion reignites the inner disk assembly of Malin 1](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12177)
*Manish Kataria,Kanak Saha*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: Malin 1的内盘存在多个恒星形成区，其中远紫外团块表现出运动学解耦和极低金属丰度，表明其由外来原始气体快速形成，支持矮星系吸积驱动中心结构演化的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Malin 1这一巨低面亮度星系中心高面亮度结构的形成机制，特别是其内部恒星形成活动是否受外部气体吸积影响。

Method: 结合AstroSat远紫外成像与MUSE积分场光谱数据，分析内10 kpc区域恒星形成复合体的空间分布、运动学特征及恒星族群性质。

Result: 发现四个恒星形成复合体，其中远紫外团块具有显著速度偏移和高气体弥散，且含有年轻、极低金属丰度（[M/H]≈-1.69）和α元素富集的恒星群体，与其周围富金属ISM明显不同。这些区域在空间和速度上分离但年龄同步、化学均一，提示来自高倾角轨道上瓦解的富气矮星系的气体吸积。

Conclusion: Malin 1中心约14 kpc范围内的高面亮度结构通过外部富气矮星系的离散吸积事件形成，促进了其复杂混合盘结构的演化。

Abstract: We present a detailed kinematic and stellar population analysis of the inner disk of Malin 1, a giant low surface brightness (GLSB) galaxy with a prominent SB0-type central morphology. AstroSat far-UV imaging reveals clumpy emission features indicating recent star formation. Using MUSE integral field spectroscopy, we identify four star-forming complexes (SFCs) within the inner 10 kpc, each associated with localized ionized gas emission in distinct H$α$ velocity channels. Two of the SFCs, including a far-UV clump, appear on the blue-shifted side ($V_{Hα}=-230~\mathrm{kms^{-1}}$), while the other two are redshifted. The far-UV clump shows a strong velocity offset ($\sim150~\mathrm{kms^{-1}}$) and high gas dispersion ($\sim250~\mathrm{kms^{-1}}$), indicating that it is kinematically decoupled from the rotating disk. The spatial and velocity isolation of these features in the channel map confirms they do not follow regular disk rotation.
  The far-UV clump hosts young (250-500 Myr), extremely metal-poor ([M/H]$\simeq$ -1.69) and $α$-enriched ($[α/Fe] \sim 0.5$) stellar populations, sharply contrasting with the surrounding super-solar gas-phase metallicity. The young stellar populations in each SFC are chemically distinct (similar to the far-UV clump) from the enriched central ISM, indicating rapid, local star formation from primitive gas before efficient mixing with the enriched ISM. Their spatial and velocity segregation, age synchronicity, and chemical homogeneity suggest an origin of gas delivered by a disrupted, gas-rich dwarf on a high-inclination (off-plane) orbit. These results suggest that the central HSB within $\rm \sim 9^{\prime\prime} (14\ kpc)$ radius component of Malin 1 has grown through discrete, externally driven accretion, contributing to its complex, hybrid disk morphology.

### [43] [Metallicity Effects on Machine Learning Classification of Dusty Stellar Sources in the Magellanic Clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12210)
*Sepideh Ghaziasgar,Mahdi Abdollahi,Atefeh Javadi,Jacco Th. van Loon,Iain McDonald,Joana Oliveira,Habib G. Khosroshahi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究利用SAGE项目的光谱数据，采用概率随机森林（PRF）分类器对大、小麦哲伦云（LMC和SMC）中的五类尘埃星源进行分类，探究环境金属丰度对机器学习模型性能的影响。结果表明，尽管LMC和SMC金属丰度不同，但模型在两者中的分类准确率相近（SMC为93%，LMC为88%），且交叉训练效果稳定，说明金属丰度对分类性能影响不大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在验证环境金属丰度是否影响机器学习模型在 dusty 恒星源分类中的表现，特别是跨星系应用的可行性。

Method: 使用SAGE项目的光谱标记数据，训练并评估了四种不同策略下的概率随机森林（PRF）分类器：分别在LMC和SMC上训练、排除PAGB类、合并数据集训练以及交叉星系统训练测试。

Result: 模型在SMC上达到93%准确率，在LMC上为88%；排除样本稀少的PAGB类后，两者均提升至92%；合并或交叉训练效果相似，显示金属丰度影响不显著。LMC与SMC的绝对星等-颜色图也显示其恒星群落相似。

Abstract: Differences in metallicity between the Large Magellanic Cloud (LMC) and the Small Magellanic Cloud (SMC) offer an opportunity to examine whether environmental metallicity affects the performance of machine learning models in classifying dusty stellar sources. The five stellar classes studied include young stellar objects (YSOs), red supergiants (RSGs), post-asymptotic giant branch stars (PAGBs), and oxygen- and carbon-rich asymptotic giant branch stars (OAGBs and CAGBs), which are key phases of stellar evolution involved in dust production. Using spectroscopically labeled data from the Surveying the Agents of Galaxy Evolution (SAGE) project, we trained and evaluated a probabilistic random forest (PRF) classifier with four approaches: (1) separate training on LMC and SMC, including all five classes, (2) excluding the underpopulated PAGB class, (3) combined LMC and SMC datasets, and (4) cross-galaxy training and testing. The model achieved 93\% accuracy on the SMC and 88\% on the LMC across all five classes. In the SMC, PAGB sources were misclassified as YSOs, mainly because of their small sample size (4 objects). When PAGB was excluded, both the LMC and the SMC reached 92\% accuracy. A combined dataset produced the same accuracy, and cross-galaxy training yielded similar results, indicating that metallicity does not significantly impact model performance. A comparison of absolute CMDs for the LMC and SMC confirms their similarity in stellar populations. These findings suggest that environmental metallicity has little effect on ML-based classification of dusty stellar sources, supporting the use of combined datasets and cross-galaxy models in low-metallicity environments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We use $^{12}$CO (J=1-0) MWISP data to study turbulence in a segment of the Local Arm. Velocity slices at different kinematic distances show similar spatial power spectra (SPSs) and structure functions (SFs), demonstrating that the entire region forms a single turbulent field with a cascade extending from $\sim 400$ pc to sub-parsec scales. The SPS slopes of both the intensity and velocity fields exhibit a systematic scale dependence that approaches the values expected from turbulence models. Cloud-to-cloud VSFs follow similar trends to the pixel-by-pixel VSFs in the extended self-similarity (ESS) scaling, indicating that velocity differences among clouds arise from large-scale turbulent motions. Velocity- and intensity-increment maps reveal filamentary, intermittent structures. The PDFs of the velocity increments display strong non-Gaussianity and are well fitted by the normal inverse gaussian (NIG) distribution, whereas the intensity increments show much weaker tails.   <summary>Details</summary>

The model accruacy matches current non-spectroscopic methods for stellar mass and redshift, surpasses them for SFR and metallicity, and introduces the first probabilistic central black hole mass estimates from imaging + photometry. It also delivers probabilistic estimates of H$α$, H$β$, [N~\textsc{ii}], and [O~\textsc{iii}] emission line fluxes directly from imaging, enabling SFR, metallicity, dust, and AGN/shock diagnostics without spectroscopy. ### [46] [Made-to-Measure Outperforms Schwarzschild's Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12425)
*Richard J. Long*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 比较了Syer和Tremaine的逐次逼近法与Schwarzschild轨道叠加法在恒星动力学建模中的性能，发现前者在低轨道数下更快且能有效重现观测数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估并比较两种经典恒星动力学建模方法在有限轨道数下的表现差异，特别是在数据重现能力、轨道分类和计算效率方面的优劣。

Method: 使用8000条轨道，在不同观测数据集和初始条件下，对比逐次逼近法（made-to-measure）与轨道叠加法的χ²拟合效果、轨道分类一致性及计算耗时。

Result: 两种方法均能实现χ²≈1或更小的数据拟合；逐次逼近法速度快3到5倍；相同初始条件下轨道分类相似但轨道权重不同；不同初始条件导致分类结果差异。

Conclusion: 逐次逼近法在效率上显著优于轨道叠加法，适合大规模星系巡天分析，但两种方法的结果依赖于初始条件，且轨道权重不具唯一性。

Abstract: Syer and Tremaine's made-to-measure method and Schwarzschild's orbit superposition method are well-known within the field of stellar dynamical modeling. This research is concerned with assessing and comparing the operational capabilities of the two methods and, in particular, the impact on observable reproduction, orbit classifications and computer elapsed times when using low orbit numbers (8000 orbits) with different observational data sets and initial conditions. Both methods are able to reproduce observed data with mean $χ^2 \approx 1$ or less. However, the made-to-measure process does so three to five times faster than the orbit superposition method, and this starts to make the made-to-measure process attractive for analyzing galaxy surveys. For a given set of initial conditions, both methods produce similar orbit classifications but the orbits behind the classifications are not the same. Orbits which are common do not have the same weights. Different initial conditions result in different classifications.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigated the influence of Active Galactic Nuclei (AGN) feedback on star formation in red spiral galaxies by analyzing a sample of 324 red and 273 blue face-on spirals selected from 115 low-redshift galaxy clusters. This multi-wavelength dataset combines optical emission line data from the Sloan Digital Sky Survey with X-ray fluxes from Chandra and XMM-Newton X-ray space telescopes. Using diagnostic emission line ratios, we constructed Baldwin-Phillips-Terlevich (BPT) diagrams, introduced in 1981 to classify galaxies based on nuclear activity. Our analysis reveals that most red spirals exhibit AGN or low-ionization nuclear emission-line region (LINER) signatures, based on optical data, as determined by their location in the BPT, Cid Fernandes, and Mazzolari diagrams. These results are consistent with the presence of negative feedback from AGNs quenching star formation. Conversely, X-ray analysis reveals that many blue spirals exhibit high X-ray luminosities and are situated in the AGN region of emission line ratio diagrams, suggesting that AGN-driven positive feedback may be enhancing star formation. Our findings support the hypothesis that AGN feedback plays a key role in the evolution of spiral galaxies, particularly in quenching star formation and driving the transition from blue to red spiral systems.

### [48] [Sub-millimeter galaxies in hierarchical models: revisiting the need for a top-heavy stellar initial mass function with Bayesian optimisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12550)
*Edward Elliott,C. M. Baugh,Cedric Lacey*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用贝叶斯优化方法，在GALFORM半解析模型的15维参数空间中进行高效搜索，并测试两种模型变体：一种采用通用的Chabrier IMF，另一种允许星暴中的IMF斜率作为自由参数变化，以评估其对三个关键观测约束的拟合能力。

Result: 当采用通用Chabrier IMF时，无法找到能同时拟合z=0 K波段光度函数、850μm SMG计数和SMG红移分布的参数组合；而允许星暴中存在偏重IMF时，模型可极好地同时拟合所有观测约束，最佳拟合的IMF斜率参数x≈0.7。

Abstract: The properties of high-redshift sub-millimetre galaxies (SMGs) remain controversial within hierarchical structure formation models. We revisit whether a top-heavy stellar initial mass function (IMF) in starbursts is required to reproduce both SMG observations and local galaxy properties. Using Bayesian optimisation, we perform an extensive search of the 15-dimensional parameter space of the GALFORM semi-analytical model. This efficient approach converges to optimal parameter values in fewer than 200 model evaluations, representing orders of magnitude fewer runs than traditional methods. We test whether GALFORM can simultaneously match three key observational constraints: the $z=0$ $K$-band luminosity function, the SMG number counts at 850~$μ$m, and the SMG redshift distribution. We consider two model variants: one with a universal solar neighbourhood IMF for all star formation, and another allowing the IMF slope in starbursts to vary as a free parameter. When assuming a universal Chabrier IMF, we find no parameter combination that simultaneously reproduces all three datasets. The model either matches the SMG constraints while grossly overpredicting the local $K$-band luminosity function, or matches the local luminosity function while severely underpredicting SMG counts by factors of 3--100. In contrast, allowing a top-heavy IMF in starbursts enables excellent simultaneous fits to all constraints. The best-fitting model prefers an IMF slope parameter $x \approx 0.7$ (where d$n$/dlog$m \propto m^{-x}$), somewhat more top-heavy than recent models but less extreme than early proposals. Our comprehensive parameter space exploration definitively confirms that, within the GALFORM framework, a top-heavy IMF in starbursts is necessary to reconcile high-redshift dusty star-forming galaxies with local galaxy populations.

### [49] [Near-infrared [P II] and [Fe II] line mapping of Galactic supernova remnants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12891)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 超新星中磷的产量或分布存在显著差异，支持其在爆发过程中不对称释放的可能性；部分观测结果可能受镍发射干扰，需进一步区分元素贡献。

Abstract: Phosphorus (P) is one of the key ingredients for life, yet its origins in galaxies remain poorly understood. In order to investigate the production of P by supernovae, we performed near-infrared (IR) [P II] and [Fe II] line mapping of 26 Galactic supernova remnants (SNRs) with the Infrared Survey Facility and Kanata telescopes, using the narrow-band filters tuned to these lines. By combining our data with archival [Fe II] maps from UKIRT, we detected both the [P II] and [Fe II] emissions in five SNRs, only the [Fe II] emission in 15 SNRs, and no line emissions in the remaining six. Using the observed [P II]/[Fe II] ratios and upper limits for non-detections, we derived the P/Fe abundance ratios, which vary by up to two orders of magnitude among our sample SNRs. This suggests that the production rate of P and/or the degree of dust destruction may differ from remnant to remnant, the latter being due to the fact that P is volatile while Fe is mostly locked in dust grains. We used the mid- and far-IR maps to examine the dust content for the five SNRs where both the line emissions are detected. As a result, we find that high P/Fe abundance ratios in the northern and southeastern regions of Cassiopeia A and the Crab Nebula, respectively, are not likely due to dust destruction but may reflect an asymmetric ejection of P during supernova explosions. In the Crab Nebula, it is also possible that near-IR [Ni II] emission contaminates the observed flux in the southeastern region, suggesting that the Ni/Fe abundance ratio, rather than the P/Fe abundance ratio, is relatively high in this part of the remnant.

### [50] [AGN feedback in merging galaxies with a SMUGGLE multiphase ISM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.13024)
*Aneesh Sivasankaran,Laura Blecha,Paul Torrey,Luke Zoltan Kelley,Aklant Bhowmick,Mark Vogelsberger,Lars Hernquist,Federico Marinacci,Laura V. Sales*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本论文通过高分辨率流体动力学模拟研究了合并星系中活动星系核（AGN）反馈驱动的快速核风，发现AGN反馈与并合动力学的协同效应在银河系类星系并合中最显著，而在Sbc型和SMC类星系中作用较弱，且低质量黑洞在SMC类星系中存在显著游荡现象。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用SMUGGLE模型结合高分辨率流体模拟，显式建模多相星际介质，并使用子网格动力摩擦处理大质量黑洞，同时利用超拉格朗日加密方案解析AGN反馈在10-100 pc尺度上的耦合过程。

Result: 在银河系类并合中AGN风主导能量并携带更多气体；Sbc类星系直到并合后期恒星形成下降时才受AGN显著影响；SMC类星系中低质量黑洞因多相ISM导致显著游荡，吸积和反馈可忽略。

Abstract: We study fast nuclear winds driven by Active Galactic Nucleus (AGN) feedback in merging galaxies using high-resolution hydrodynamics simulations. We use Stars and MUltiphase Gas in GaLaxiEs (SMUGGLE) to explicitly model the multiphase interstellar medium (ISM) and employ sub-grid dynamical friction for massive black holes (BHs). Furthermore, we use a super-Lagrangian refinement scheme to resolve AGN feedback coupling to the ISM at $\sim10-100\,$pc scales. By comparison between merging and isolated galaxies, with and without AGN feedback, we identify trends in the complex interplay between dynamics, BH fueling and feedback, and star formation and feedback. We consider three galaxy types: Milky Way analogs, Sbc-type galaxies, and Small Magellanic Cloud (SMC) analogs. The synergy between AGN feedback and merger dynamics is strongest in the Milky Way-like mergers, where the AGN winds are energetically dominant and entrain more gas when the initially thin disks become thick and amorphous during the merger. In contrast, the merger of thicker, vigorously star-forming Sbc galaxies is not strongly impacted by AGN feedback until star formation declines in the post-merger phase. Finally, while the sub-grid dynamical friction prescription effectively retains BHs in galactic nuclei during more massive mergers, the clumpy multiphase ISM induces significant wandering of low-mass BHs $\mathrm{(<10^5M_\odot)}$ in the shallow potentials of the SMC-like galaxies. These low-mass BHs wander at distances $\gtrsim 2$ kpc from the galactic center, yielding negligible BH accretion and feedback. This has implications for LISA event rates and present a further challenge to understanding the rapid growth of $z\sim7-10$ quasars discovered by JWST.

### [51] [Infrared photometry and CaT spectroscopy of the most metal-poor in-situ globular cluster VVV-CL001](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.13161)
*W. Haro Moya,C. Moni Bidin,M. C. Parisi,D. Geisler,M. Blaña,S. Villanova,F. Mauro,A. -N. Chené,R. E. Cohen,S. Ramírez Alegría,R. Contreras Ramos,M. Zoccali,C. Muñoz,B. Dias*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: VVV-CL001是银河系内晕中一个古老且金属丰度极低的球状星团，通过结合光谱、天体测量和近红外测光数据，研究确认其年龄约为121亿年，金属丰度[Fe/H] = -2.25，距离太阳约7.1 kpc。其轨道高度偏心，受银河系核球影响，起源于银河系早期原位形成，可能是被星系棒捕获的原始盘族星团遗迹，为研究银河系早期演化提供了重要线索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究银河系核球区域难以观测的球状星团VVV-CL001的基本参数及其形成起源，以揭示银河系早期化学和动力学演化历史。

Method: 结合FORS2/VLT中分辨率光谱（用于测量金属丰度和视向速度）、Gaia DR3自行数据、FourStar/Magellan近红外测光（用于精确定位星团中心、结构及测光参数），综合分析其基本性质和轨道特征。

Result: 确定VVV-CL001为一个古老（12.1^{+1.0}_{-1.2} Gyr）、极贫金属（[Fe/H] = -2.25 ± 0.05）、距离7.1 kpc的星团，具有高偏心率轨道（e=0.76），轨道范围在银河系内区（R<5 kpc），最大垂直距离约1 kpc，自行和视向速度分别为μ_α^* = -3.68 mas/yr，μ_δ = -1.76 mas/yr，v_r = -334 km/s。

Conclusion: VVV-CL001很可能起源于银河系早期的原位形成，属于被星系棒捕获的原始盘族星团，是银河系最早期组装阶段的化石遗迹之一，对理解银河系早期演化具有重要意义。

Abstract: Globular clusters in the Galactic bulge are difficult to study due to high extinction and severe crowding. VVV-CL001 is an old, metal-poor, and fast cluster in the inner bulge, whose extreme properties make it a key probe of the early chemical and dynamical evolution of the Milky Way. We derive its fundamental parameters by combining spectroscopy, astrometry, and near-infrared photometry. Metallicity and radial velocity were measured from medium-resolution FORS2/VLT spectra; proper motions from Gaia DR3; and FourStar/Magellan photometry was used to refine the cluster centre, derive its structure, and estimate age, distance, and reddening. VVV-CL001 is confirmed to be an old ($12.1^{+1.0}_{-1.2}$ Gyr), metal-poor ($[\text{Fe}/\text{H}] = -2.25 \pm 0.05$) cluster at a heliocentric distance of $7.1^{+1.3}_{-1.1}$ kpc, with reddening $E(J-K_s) = 1.40^{+0.01}_{-0.02}$. Its mean proper motions are $μ_α^* = -3.68 \pm 0.09$ and $μ_δ= -1.76 \pm 0.10$ mas yr$^{-1}$, and its radial velocity is $-334 \pm 4$ km s$^{-1}$. The orbit is eccentric ($e = 0.76^{+0.10}_{-0.14}$), confined to the inner Galaxy ($|Z|_{\max} \approx 1$ kpc) and within the bar's influence ($R < 5$ kpc), with pericentre $0.6^{+0.3}_{-0.2}$ kpc and apocentre $4.5^{+2.5}_{-1.2}$ kpc. Its old age, low metallicity, and orbital properties support an in-situ origin, identifying VVV-CL001 as one of the most metal-poor inner-Galaxy clusters formed in the early Milky Way. It likely belongs to the primordial disk cluster population later trapped by the bar, making it a fossil remnant of the earliest phases of Galactic assembly.
